You are wise.   
If the dragon doesn't even know where he is going yet, how can we?   
He likes to hang out there, the 200ema and the pivot (thick yellow line). It is must be like a shady spot under a tree near a babbling brook or something.  
Also it is getting toward lunch time NY. Trading can be thin then as the institutional traders (the ones that trade big lots, millions) go out to eat their lunches. Personally I don't like to trade after 11:30am or 12 noon (est) unless there is some special data release scheduled, like FOMC...   
Trading is exciting and we like the excitement. But if the dragon isn't moving in a decisive way what is there to trade? He sleeping under a tree dreaming of going here and there and the dss is going all over the place and he isn't moving at all.   
We can't wake him up just because we want to trade. We have to wait until he gets up on his own and we just have to be ready.

  * [#226](/thread/post/3515543#post3515543 "Post Permalink")

  * Mar 3, 2010 3:52pm  Mar 3, 2010 3:52pm 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar96047_66.gif) jiva34](jiva34)

  * Joined Mar 2009 | Status: Just visiting | [12,891 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=96047)

Dragon up against long term trend line  
macd on all the time frames up to 1h have all turned over  
1hr getting ready to.  
dss heading down from over bought..  
  
h4 is questionable and suggest upside could still prevails...   
but the dss can go up and the dragon may not move or even sometimes he actually goes down. It is more or less measuring "what he is thinking" not necessarily what he is doing. He's a little schizophrenic that way..  
So why do I like dss?  
I like dss because for one thing dss can help to identify the trend.   
For instance is dss is going down like anything but the dragon is only moving slightly down, then it is most like a retracement not a reversal. And if dss is going up like anything and the dragon is going up like anything, that's the trend..  
The dss on this 4hr looks to me like consolidation. And a move back down is likely... moves up are equaling moves down both for the range of the dragon's movements and for dss...  
Anyway I entered short.  
I'm taking a target of the 200ema on the 5m.  
Almost open for European mkts.  
since Asia took thing up, possible Frankfurt open will take things down a bit..  
The neg divegence on the 15m says the move may be good for at least the 200ema on the 5m.

I would like to see if we could work a bit more into filtering bad trades and "when to trade/not to trade" when to "Enter the trade when not to"  
>    
>  Thanks again Jiva
> 
> Ignored

Yes. This is the question. We all would like to know that answer perfectly.  
  
Trading is a skill. It takes practice. Like any skill, the basics are learned first.  
  
Say with golf. How to stand. How to hold the club. How to measure the wind. The condition of the grass. The distance. The proper club, etc. etc etc. And ssshh don't talk on the tee.  
  
So how to know when to enter and when to exit.  
What I am using with a certain amount of success is following the dragon as he moves through the different time frames. If I see a set up on the 1 min I want to know is this just a hiccup or is he taking deep deep breath and about to embark.  
So I look at the where he is on the 5m. Is he about to go the other way from the 1m, then I might want to see his behavior on the 15m. And in this way try to put together a better idea of where he trying to go.  
  
This take practice. To flip through the time frames. Eventually it makes sense. Sometimes I am more interested in the 1m and the 5m and sometimes I give the 1m and 15m more attention. Things get really interesting when I start looking at 30m, 1hr, 4hr, etc.   
  
He does not move in a straight line. To look at just one time frame is linear, his moves are what is called curvilinear. So different cross sections of time can capture this curvileanar move wheareas just one time frame is 2 dimensional, multi time frames helps to get multi-dimensions.   
  
A book by JM Hurst one of the fathers of tech analysis written in the early 1900's (when calculations were all done by abacus and on fingers and toes) is very enlightening about this. Mr. Hurst was not a trader per se. He was a physicist and he used physics to analyze markets.   
He discusses this multi time frame aspect in great detail. It really open my eyes to charting in a whole new way.  
  
Recommended reading....books by JM Hurst..  
  
Some of the recent trades have been documented with screenshots showing somewhat the use of the time frames.  
  
Eventually the fog clear and a continuum becomes evident. Practice and more practice. Sleeping on it. Dreaming about it. voila.. Oh I see... 

[0 ](javascript:void\(0\);) [0 ](javascript:void\(0\);)

So many things to consider...  
  
In looking at r1 as a target I neglected to consider how sometimes the r or s from the previous day is as far as the dragon will go. It doesn't happen all the time but it happens enough times to make it something that needs to be considered when setting a target.  
  
He has gone to r1 from yesterday _and it just so happens that's exactly where I entered._![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f62b.png?v=15.1)

If I feel the need to trade, I can use a demo or run the simulator just to keep active and awake...  
I really have to work at avoiding overtrading. It's a trap I've fallen into more than I care to admit.

  * Mar 5, 2010 6:41pm  Mar 5, 2010 6:41pm 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar96047_66.gif) jiva34](jiva34)

  * Joined Mar 2009 | Status: Just visiting | [12,891 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=96047)

The shi channels take a little getting used to but they can be very helpful.  
They do shift as he moves but they do that becasue they are following the trend and the short term trend changes, so they change. But the channels help to identify possible turning points.   
When the dragon is as an outer trend line he very often turns back, if he breaks out the trend lines will change in a little while to identify the new direction. The dashed median line is important. He will test that median and it also can be turning point.  
If the shi lines intersect with 200ema, ot a pivot, sup or res or trend line etc it can be especially significant.  
Just sensitive areas to give a little extra attention to. Not necessarily definite signals, just something to be a little attentive to.   
(Don't ask me what _shi_ _channels means, haven't the foggiest.)

Trading the EURUSD for the last several months has been great. When the market went up EURUSD went up, when the market went down EURUSD went down. Pretty much tick for tick. But that correlation is breaking.   
Market goes up EURUSD goes down. Or goes up or goes nowhere.   
I was using equities movements to help gauge EURUSD but probably not anymore or at least not in the same way.  
  
Data is light this week. What will drive the market? News? ECB,FED comments?  
We shall see.   
  
In trying to identify a longer term trend so that scalping can be done in line with a trend here's what I am seeing. I will watch this for a while to see if I have it right and if so look to enter accordingly on the 1m.  
  
I would be looking for a trade just before or around Frankfurt open...

  * Joined Mar 2009 | Status: Just visiting | [12,891 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=96047)

Had a couple of decent trades. Nothing to write home about..  
But then late morning I wanted to catch the dragon short as he headed for the pivot. The trades are not in mt4 which I use for finding setups but are placed in an account that has a page with all the pairs on it, unbelievable, I sold the wrong pair..................................................![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f633.png?v=15.1)  
I wanted to sell EURUSD instead I hit the wrong button and sold GBPUSD at the very bottom of its run...  
By the time I figured out what had happened it was already -25 pips..  
Rode it out for a while and took the loss, -25 pips. If I had kept it over Asian session it would have been +25 but I didn't want to leave a position open if I couldn't monitor it.   
That's not the first time I've hit the wrong button on that trading page.   
As if trading isn't difficult enough just trying to decipher the charts then there is all the technical stuff, like brokers site jamming, hitting the wrong button, power outages, time out disconnects.... Yikes...  
It's the Wild West...  

[http://t3.gstatic.com/images?q=tbn:m.../wild_west.jpg](http://t3.gstatic.com/images?q=tbn:mXlvt7teAaBNMM:http://www.tagate.com/western/wild_west.jpg)

  * Edited 5:06am  Mar 10, 2010 4:54am | Edited 5:06am 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar96047_66.gif) jiva34](jiva34)

  * Joined Mar 2009 | Status: Just visiting | [12,891 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=96047)

Here's what I look for.  
The 5m shows the macd cross and the alignment with dss that occurred a little while back.  
There is a trend line and 200ema that have acted a strong resistance on the 15m.  
But also in the 15m the same aligning is taking place with macd and dss..  
So even if the 5m retraces a little there is no need toe exit since this is showing a move down on the 15 now... As the 15m plays out, by the same logic attention would turn to the 30m to see if the down move will carry over there, if so then follow the move there and check later on with the 1hr etc..  
  
_note: I placed a sell order at the bottom (my specialty![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f61c.png?v=15.1)) earlier today..   
I just kept it in place anyway and didn't take a stopout. I have a few longer term (weeks) positions anyway and just added it to the others since I see EURUSD ultimately as a short for the next few months._

  * Mar 10, 2010 5:15am  Mar 10, 2010 5:15am 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar96047_66.gif) jiva34](jiva34)

  * Joined Mar 2009 | Status: Just visiting | [12,891 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=96047)

This is playing out perfectly.  
The 15m now shows a downward trend, the 1m is retracing, and the 5m is in no man's land, could retrace or could continue down...  
the shi channels are helpful here.  
On the 15m the dragon has retreated from resistance at the upper shi channel/200 ema/trendline he will head for the median between the channels   
when he reaches the median he will consider again should he go back up and head for the upper channel again or cross the median and head for the lower channel...  
_This is a very likely scenario._ _Reminder nothing is set in stone!!!_

  * Joined Mar 2009 | Status: Just visiting | [12,891 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=96047)

Storytime:  
About complicating things:  
(Old Bengali-mother story...)  
  
The wife was complaining. Our house is too small. We need more room. The husband says I do not have so much money to make a bigger house. The wife complaining, complaining, complaining. The household was not peaceful because of the complaining.  
  
He went to his guru, "Oh, maharaja, please help me. I have no peace. House not big enough, house too small.. All the time complaining. What can I do?"  
Guru asks, "Do you have a cow?"  
"Yes, we have a cow."  
"Then put the cow in the house."  
"In the house?"  
"Yes, in the house."  
At home the wife is in disbelief, "In the house?"  
"Yes, guru maharaja's answer was, put the cow in the house."  
So, they put the cow in the house.  
What a mess. Big cow, in the house.  

[http://t0.gstatic.com/images?q=tbn:W...nSwissHead.jpg](http://t0.gstatic.com/images?q=tbn:Wh1kY9rq7AwJmM:http://www.larryschultzartist.com/Cow%2520Original/BrownSwissHead.jpg)  

  
The man returned to the guru, "Maharaja, it is not solving the problem.Problem is worse."  
Guru asks, "Does the cow have a calf?"  
"Yes, the cow has a calf."  
"Then put the calf in the house too."  
The wife is astounded. "The calf in the house too? Are you sure you are hearing guru maharaja properly? Maybe you are misunderstanding."  
"No, he definitely said to put the calf in the house too."  
It didn't take long for the man to return to the guru.   
"Did that solve the problem?"  
"No, no it is much worse. It is an impossible situation!"  

[http://t1.gstatic.com/images?q=tbn:V...w-and-calf.jpg](http://t1.gstatic.com/images?q=tbn:VjahrqRbwdmTGM:http://warkscol.files.wordpress.com/2008/03/mother-cow-and-calf.jpg)  

"Good. Now take the cow and the calf out of the house."  
So when he went home and they took the cow and the calf out of the house, the wife sighed, "Oh this is wonderful, so much room now."

dss is already overbought and macd has only now crossed  
I have not made a mental note of this type of configuration although I have seen it before. So I will monitor it to see if my suspicion is correct, that there is not much of an upside move to this... so for the future I may be able make a decision with some confidence.

Turns out a long position was good on the setup. I hesitated because dss was so far into overbought before macd crossed. But macd was far below 0 so I will make a mental note of it and see if that is a configuration that can be traded on in the future.  
Overthinking is trap, but I want to take as much of the gamble out of it as I can without crippling myself with too much cerebral functioning.  
If it is a configuration that can be counted on then that will take the cerebral strain out of the next time.  
Will be looking for a possible fresh short set up...

Notusing them seems would be like driving on a highway with no road markings or exit signs...

problem is  
Even though there has been a neg macd divergence with dragon setup,  
the macd divergence has been a little compromised.  
  
when a divergence occurs but the macd touches 0 or crosses to the other side of the zero line and back again, it tends to neutralize the affect of a divergence.  
  
there is a dragon set up for short. but the trend is up.  
What to do?

charts as clean as i do, you con remove heiken ashi smoothed from your

it crosses it (i use bolinger bands with the center line highlighted)

Great job and keep up the good work.

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar96047_66.gif) jiva34](jiva34)

  * Joined Mar 2009 | Status: Just visiting | [12,891 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=96047)

So many lessons. To stop trading would be for me to stop living.  
Lesson today. (Perhaps the lessons learned are the real value gained.)  

**RESPECT**  

Whenever I forget to show respect and appreciation for the dragon I run into problems...   
It is a relationship. I must learn to be happy with whatever the dragon allows me. The tendency is to try to take more and override the dragon.. No No...   
Doesn't work like that.   
Dragon will give. I cannot force or disrespect. He will show me if I am in the right state of mind. If not. I get kick..... Smacked. Run over. .. Pulverized.  
And otherwise beat up...  
I can't see a thing on the template. None of it makes any sense.   

Respect  
Respect  
Respect  

Such an important lesson. Who would have thought respect would be so important in trading. It is...  
When I don't show it that's when I realize how important respect is.  
Without respect I am blind. Respect acts like a window into another dimension.   
_Without respect I am denied access. It is very subtle. But undeniable._  
re·spect (r<http://img.tfd.com/hm/GIF/ibreve.gif>-sp<http://img.tfd.com/hm/GIF/ebreve.gif>kt<http://img.tfd.com/hm/GIF/prime.gif>)_tr.v._ **re·spect·ed** , **re·spect·ing** , **re·spects** **1.** To feel or show deferential regard for; esteem.  
**2.** To avoid violation of or interference with: respect the speed limit.  
**3.** To relate or refer to; concern.  
  
_n._**1.** A feeling of appreciative, often deferential regard; esteem. See Synonyms at [regard](http://www.thefreedictionary.com/regard).  
**2.** The state of being regarded with honor or esteem.  
**3.** Willingness to show consideration or appreciation.  
**4.** **respects** Polite expressions of consideration or deference: pay one's respects.  
**5.** A particular aspect, feature, or detail: In many respects this is an important decision.  
**6.** _Usage Problem_ Relation; reference. See Usage Note at [regard](http://www.thefreedictionary.com/regard).  
  

**_My trading desk on days when I forget to respect the dragon  
_**

(Actually taking a nap the first time and eating breakfast in the other room the second time.)  
Total between the 2 about 60 pips. I know if I had been watching with laser focus, it never would have been 60 pips... Fear. I might lose the little gains that started to show up...  
Will see about making this part of my trading strategy. Set it and go..  
Come back later...   
At least for some of the set ups....

Just a whole bunch of little ones.  
I read and study some of the other threads and systems. Try 'em out a bit.  
But I just keep coming back to the dragon.  
Have added 2 ma's and removed the 3 I was using.  
red is a 10 ema, and blue is 50 ema.  
The red 10ema cross of ashi smoothed is significant for trend change.  
Watching the interplay between the 2 ma's can be instructive. Help to stay in a trend.   
The further they are apart the more likely the end of the trend is approaching.  
the closer they are together the more likely a big move is coming.  
I will be watching how they act over the next little while in relation to the dragon's meanderings.   
And there is always the cross that confirms a trend is beginning.   
More on the ma's later.

  * [#364](/thread/post/3552556#post3552556 "Post Permalink")

  * Mar 16, 2010 2:20am  Mar 16, 2010 2:20am 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar96047_66.gif) jiva34](jiva34)

  * Joined Mar 2009 | Status: Just visiting | [12,891 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=96047)

There's so much more to successful trading, not the least of which is money management. Stop losses, position sizing, etc.  
  
Just being right about a trade is actually not enough. Because there will always be some bad trades, no matter how good a trader is.   
  
**Managing loss is the key to success._It is the cost of doing a trading business._**  
  
Trading the 1m I do not like to take more than a 10pip loss. If my entries are good then a 10pip stop loss should be more than sufficient.  
  
More than a 10pip loss is very difficult to make back trading the 1m. It would take several trades just to break even. To average between 5 and 10 pips gain is very acceptable on the 1m. So to take more than a 10 pip loss is a real setback.   
  
But to take the loss and move on is necessary. If the trade was not what I had estimated it to be, I want to get out.   
  
Part of deciding to enter a trade should always be to consider the stop loss. Is it worth it? Can I place a 10 pip sl safely?   
  
I only want to pay a possible 10pips to enter.   
  
I can't afford more than that... That's the budget... 

[0 ](javascript:void\(0\);) [0 ](javascript:void\(0\);)

1st trade of the day.  
A new calm has come over me for trading.  
By following the 10pip stop loss rule.  
Could things be that simple?  
that all the stress and anxiety can be so easily eliminated by strictly following the 10 pip rule?  
I think so.  
If the system is good, then the signals will be good the majority of the time.   
If the signal turned out to be false then get out...

stopped out.  
I need to be careful of:  
not waiting ofr the 1m to give the actual signal.  
I need to remember and not get ahead of myself, that I only have 10 pips in the budget for a stop loss. If I take a signal on higher time frame 10 pips most likely will not be enough and I will get stopped out.  
So the actual signal has to be on the 1m even if I see all sorts of signals on the 30m or 15m. They can only help to support a signal on the 1m.   
But with 10 pips in mo pocket to buy a trade the signal has to be on the 1m.  
The screen shot shows how I got carried away with what I saw on the 30min. But did not wait for an entry on the 1m.  
The cost of educations...  
  
  
has some retracing to do.  
If I see the signal on the 1min will go back in short.

I don't know if anyone else has this or not, but I think I have some sort of weird phobia.  
I do very well trading short, but long positions I either just don't see them or misread them, and even have a kind of fear of them. It's very strange indeed.  
  
How to shake it I'm not sure have been dealing with it for a while.  
I prefer to trade EURUSD but if the trend is up it doesn;t work.  
  
What I may have to do is switch to USDCHF for short trades.  
Until I can see how to get rid of this phobia.  
Fear of heights?  
It's totally silly because trading pairs means one is always short against the other. So up is down and down is up all the time. It must be some visual problem...  
Anyway switched to USDCHF for some shorts and voila...

I was about to see a shrink, but since there are some other traders with the same symptoms, i feel relieved. Maybe it has to do with the fact that i a short rally, you see the previous high on your left on the chart and maybe your brain interprets the fact that you go short, that you are going back to earth where safety and stability is. To be honest, I have no clu.

okay here's the thing!!!!  
That makes all the difference in the world. (Whether its right side up or not..)  
Use sell stop and buy stop!!!  
the screenshot shows the buy stop order that was not filled but the sell stop order that was and went on to make +30 pips.  
There was a bit of a small range bound consolidation for 3 or 4 hours.   
My head was pounding, headache to end all headaches!!  
I just set the 2 pending orders:  
Buy stop 2 pips above the top of the swing high  
and sell stop 2 pips below the swing low  
placed stops and limits at the same time and passed out.  
Woke up and voila. The sell stop had been filled and was at the tgt, just above s3...  
The dragon won't go much more than s3 or r3 on any one given day, usually....

EA looks the direction of ma and macd at 8:30est, then takes order between 9am to 10am.  
So if ma and macd are up at 8:30, EA will take long in spite of current ma and macd down.  
This is the reason why EA takes the opposite order with your posted chart.  
  
EA is only for 15m. I will change it, but it will take some time. Please wait.

  * [#386](/thread/post/3777108#post3777108 "Post Permalink")

  * Jun 4, 2010 8:16pm  Jun 4, 2010 8:16pm 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar124426_2.gif) Taiyakixz](taiyakixz)

  * | Joined Nov 2009  | Status: Trader | [325 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=124426)

jiva34,  
  
EA updated.  
  
\- EA looks 5m and 1m fractals.  
\- add parameter TakeProfit  
\- add parameter LookBackBars  
\- still only for 15m chart  
  
With LookBackBars, you can set which bar EA checks the direction.  
EA checks ma and macd direction at LookBackBars earlier than starting trade hour.  
trade hour starts at 9am, and the default LookBackBars is 1.  
So EA checks ma and macd at 8:45 that is 1 bar earlier than 9am.  
If you want to use ma and macd at 9am, set to LookBackBars to 0.  
If you want to use ma and macd at 8:30, set to LookBackBars to 2.  
In case of LookBackBars 0, the direction of ma and macd can change between 9am to 9:15, take care.  
  
  
To other members,  
this EA is for test and under discussing with jiva34. Do not use it with real trade. 

Attached File(s)

![File Type: mq4](https://assets.faireconomy.media/images/attach/mq4.gif) [The Dragon EA testv2.mq4](/attachment/file/485353?d=1275650166) 8 KB | 200 downloads

macd and 10sma may be even a better combination than 197sma and 10 sma.  
may not even be necessary to add robby dss stoch... or heiken ashi..  
then again maybe adding robby dss stoch will eliminate the losing trades altogether.  
  
after adding the robby dss to the tested chart the indi did not filter out any losing trades but in fact prevented some winning trades, even after trying several different settings. I think it would confuse things.  
  
Data is released usually at 8:30 am and that can cause a significant move but sometimes there is important data released again at 10:am. So the market can reverse at 10 or just stand still at 8:30 waiting for 10. So there will be some losing trades. How to minimize losses and maximize gains. Big profit target seems to work nicely. Some of these moves can be 200 to 300 pips in a day.  
Opening 2 positions and closing one after reasonable gains will help. Like Jeoff's eav9.   
  
want to test this pair EURJPY with dragon algorithm for Jeoff's Tokyo open.   
  
would like to test GBPUSD with dragon algorithm at Tokyo open

Hi,The ea is not really ready for trading. We are trying to develop it. There's no telling why you didn't get any orders filled. GMT settings, check the journal for error messages, etc.  
I am just learning programming, very very novice. Taiyakixz is the expert doing the programming. I was getting order send error 4107, and unmatched data errors. After a little research, as I say I m just learning I was able to fix the problem which comes from the famous problems with 4 and 5 digit brokers and data history. I am posting the fixed version on the first page as v3.  
Thanks for experimenting. Feedback welcome..

  * [#403](/thread/post/3782972#post3782972 "Post Permalink")

  * Jun 7, 2010 10:58pm  Jun 7, 2010 10:58pm 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar96047_66.gif) jiva34](jiva34)

  * Joined Mar 2009 | Status: Just visiting | [12,891 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=96047)

For general reference:  
  
order send error 4107  
and  
error unmatched data entry  
  
were fixed by replacing "ask" and "bid" in the code with  
  
NormalizeDouble(Ask,Digits)  
and  
NormalizeDouble(Bid,Digits)  
respectively  
  
Tester results were completely different as many many more trades were taken  
I will be rerunning the tester for various settings and also testing the demo live.

Jiva, yes, I know where you hang around.  
  
I am also more then tired of getting glued to these monitors for so many hrs.  
In one way or another it tends to become addictive.  
Then you start seeing a trade where there is actually none, I guess out of boredom...........and then the adrenaline level goes up, and you feel part of it all again.  
  
That other EA I am testing as well, interesting, but a bit too quiet to my real liking. Still, pips are pips, and had so far 4 winners and 1 loser, which was Sunday opening of our brokers.  
  
Will set The Dragon up later this morning.  
Am using DSS already, but not as a main indi. If you don't watch it, one starts adding indis over indi and they basically do ALL the same.

I agree Geoff's indi is very good. Albeit only once a day if conditions allow.  
I am looking to set up several eas. Geoff's is definitely one of them. The dragon made into an ea will be a prize winner. I am thinking to set it for trading only during active times, mkt opens, data releases etc..   
Yes it is true, if I start to add more and more indis I know I am losing my focus. Pretty soon the chart is so cluttered I can't even see the candles. It's a disease!!  
this stoch cross is very interesting. the slow stochastic is actually a mimic of the macd default. When they cross in either overbought or oversold the signals are good, even on the 5 min which tends to be a little schizophrenic.  
Once an entry strategy is found to be reliable, then the necessity for managing the trade is there. Targets, stops, trailing stops, lot size etc. Then the ea can be coded.

1st tgt reached +20  
(not the best time to enter a trade  
mkt is slow and lunch time NY  
but if this is an ea it will go by signals and the buy signal was there.   
(unless the ea has the settings for when to buy based on time of day)  
was not at the screen when the tgt hit, so did not move stop for 2nd position. the ea would have done that and been stopped out on the 2nd position for +4.  
however the 2nd position is still open so will trail it when it goes 20 pips again...

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar96047_66.gif) jiva34](jiva34)

buy signal EURUSD 1hr  
2 positions  
1st tgt +20  
2nd tgt +40  
stop loss 120  
to trail 11 pips after 1 tgt.  
on second thought may have entered 1 bar too early. The cross should be fixed, that is the cross should be there after the bar closes.  
In this practice the bar has not closed yet. It has another 46 minutes to run, anything can happen in 46 mins...  
So the ea would not have entered long here. It will stick strictly to the rules.... The benefit of using a robot...
